//== Starting Point  (iz_int) =================================
iz_int,18,30,0	script	iz_int#intro_start	HIDDEN_WARP_NPC,6,6,{
	end;
OnTouch:
	navigateto("iz_int", 52, 30, NAV_NONE, 1); // Individual map name not required
	if (getd(".start" + strnpcinfo(1)) == 0) {
		setd ".start" + strnpcinfo(1), 1;
		initnpctimer;
		mapannounce strnpcinfo(4), "[Tip] You can move to the desired point by clicking the ground with the left mouse button.", bc_map,0xFF0000;
	}
	end;
OnTimer9000:
	mapannounce strnpcinfo(4), "[Tip] While holding down the right mouse button, drag to rotate the screen.", bc_map,0xFF0000;
	end;
OnTimer18000:
	mapannounce strnpcinfo(4), "[Tip] You can leave through the shining warp gate.", bc_map,0xFF0000;
	emotion ET_SURPRISE, getnpcid(0, "#room_out" + replacestr( strnpcinfo(4), "iz_int", "" ));
	end;
OnTimer21000:
	emotion ET_SURPRISE, getnpcid(0, "#room_out" + replacestr( strnpcinfo(4), "iz_int", "" ));
	end;
OnTimer24000:
	emotion ET_SURPRISE, getnpcid(0, "#room_out" + replacestr( strnpcinfo(4), "iz_int", "" ));
	end;
OnTimer27000:
	mapannounce strnpcinfo(4), "[Tip] Leave this area to continue.", bc_map,0xFF0000;
	stopnpctimer;
	setd ".start" + strnpcinfo(1), 0;
	end;
}
iz_int01,18,30,0	duplicate(iz_int#intro_start)	iz_int01#intro_start	HIDDEN_WARP_NPC,6,6

//== Wounded Swordsman (iz_int) =================================
iz_int,56,32,3	script	Wounded Swordsman#intro_npc01_iz_int	4_TOWER_01,5,5,{
	@intro_npc01 = 1;
	npctalk "Oh...", "", bc_self;
	classchange HIDDEN_WARP_NPC, "", bc_self;// todo: classchange self remain on map
	classchange 4_TOWER_02, "Wounded Swordsman#intro_npc02_" + strnpcinfo(4), bc_self;
	end;

OnTouch:
	if (@intro_npc01 == 0) {
		npctalk "Urgh... please... help me...", "", bc_self;
		sleep2 500;
		npctalk "In order to talk with me.. click my body..", "", bc_self;
	}
	else {// debug
		classchange HIDDEN_WARP_NPC, "", bc_self;
		classchange 4_TOWER_02, "Wounded Swordsman#intro_npc02_" + strnpcinfo(4), bc_self;
	}
	end;

OnInit:
	questinfo 21001, QTYPE_QUEST, 1, Job_Novice;
	end;
}

iz_int,56,32,3	script	Wounded Swordsman#intro_npc02_iz_int	HIDDEN_WARP_NPC,{
	if (isbegin_quest(21001) == 0) {
		mes "[Wounded]";
		mes "Wow! Thanks a lot!";
		mes "I don't know how our ship got wrecked";
		mes "but we should find the captain.";
		next;
		mes "[Wounded]";
		mes "... I may be too injured.";
		mes "Maybe you can go without me?";
		setquest 21001;
		next;
		cutin "tutorial02",4;
		mes "^4d4dff!- Information -!^000000";
		mes "NPC Quest Received.";
	}
	else {
		mes "[Wounded]";
		mes "Luckily the water has not entered the ship.";
		mes "I will wait here, you should go see the captain.";
		next;
		mes "[Wounded]";
		mes "I'm fine! I'm fine!";
		mes "Don't worry about me, you should really go to the captain!";
		next;
		mes "^4d4dff!- Information -!^000000";
	}
	mes "^4d4dffQuest info Shortcut is Alt + U^000000";
	mes "Use it anytime to check on the status of a quest.";
	close2;
	cutin "",255;
	end;

OnInit:
	questinfo 21001, QTYPE_QUEST, 1, Job_Novice;
	end;
}

// - Captain Carocc (Ship)
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
int_land,78,103,5	script	Captain Carocc#intro_npc03	4_M_REINDEER,{
	switch( isbegin_quest(21008) ) {
	case 0:
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "There are still people in the cabins?!";
		mes "At least you are safe.";
		mes "Are you alright?";
		next;
		if (select("I'm alright, but others need help.", "I think I am the last?") == 1) {
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "There are more people left?";
			mes "I will send a rescue team to them.";
			mes "Thank you for your report.";
		} else {
			mes "[Captain Carocc]";
			mes "Alright, that's good.";
			mes "The storm came unexpectedly but I never thought it would hit us that hard.";
		}
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "At least most people made it to safety.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "See the trees there? ^4d4dffFollow them to the southwest^000000 to find a new ship.";
		mes "The ship will take you to ^4d4dffIzlude^000000, our original destination.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "Ah! By the way, those ^4d4dffPorings^000000 on this island drop materials we could use for repairs.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "^4d4dffKill the Porings and bring 2 pieces of Lumber to the southern crew^000000.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "It is a hard task, but you look tough enough.";
		specialeffect2 EF_HEAL2;
		heal 9999,0;
		skilleffect 34,0;
		sc_start SC_BLESSING,240000,10;
		skilleffect 29,0;
		sc_start SC_INCREASEAGI,240000,10;
		if (isbegin_quest(21001) == 1) {
			completequest 21001;
			getexp 600,600;
		}
		setquest 21008;
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "To fight, you have to equip your gear.";
		mes "You should already have ^4d4dffweapon and armor^000000 equipped.";
		next;
		cutin "tutorial03",4;
		mes "!- Information -!";
		mes "^4d4dffYou can equip gear or use items by simply double clicking them.";
		mes "The item window can be opened by pressing Alt + E or using the menu button.^000000";
		next;
		mes "!- Information -!";
		mes "^4d4dffEquipped Items can be seen by pressing Alt + Q.";
		mes "Either double click or drag & drop to equip or unequip gear.^000000";
		next;
		cutin "",255;
		mes "[Captain Carlock]";
		mes "Did you check all your equipment?";
		mes "You should check ^4d4dffskill distribution^000000 as well.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carlock]";
		mes "For best results in battle, you should distribute your status points properly.";
		mes "^4d4dffIf you want to increase your strength, you need to raise Str^000000. ^4d4dffIf you want to increase your hit success rate, you must raise Dex, and so on.^000000.";
		break;
	case 1:
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		specialeffect2 EF_HEAL2;
		heal 9999, 0;
		skilleffect 34,0;
		sc_start SC_BLESSING,240000,10;
		skilleffect 29,0;
		sc_start SC_INCREASEAGI,240000,10;
		mes "^4d4dffThe Ship^000000 is anchored in the southwest. It will take you to Izlude.";
		mes "Don't forget to ^4d4dffget some Lumber^000000 for the ship.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "And don't forget to distribute your ^4d4dffstatus points^000000 either.";
		break;
	case 2:
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "The ship is ready to sail to Izlude.";
		mes "You can find it on south-western part of the island.";
		close;
	}
	next;
	mes "! - Information -!";
	mes "^4d4dffYou get a status bonus for every level you gain.";
	mes "The status window can be opened and closed with the shortcut Alt + A^000000.";
	next;
	mes "! - Information -!";
	mes "^4d4dffPlease properly distribute the status points you need to battle^000000.";
	next;
	mes "[Captain Carocc]";
	mes "Kill Porings and bring Lumber to the crew.";
	mes "Good luck!";
	close;

OnInit:
	questinfo 21008, QTYPE_QUEST, 1, Job_Novice;
	end;
}

		next;

		mes "That guy over there lost his memory, didn't know his own name. So I gave him a new name:";
		mes "Lumin.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "Soon we will head to Izlude where you can talk to other people like you just talked to me.";

		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "Many youngsters visit the ^4d4dffKingdom of Rune Midgard^000000 to chase their dreams.";
		mes "Izlude is a satellite city of Prontera, the capital of Rune Midgard.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "Izlude always welcomes young adventurers like you who have just started their journey through the world.";
		mes "You are one of them, of course.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "I would like to tell you more stories, but it's time to get ready.";
		mes "There is an academy in Izlude for newcomers like yourself.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "I will give you more details later. See you at the harbor deck.";
		next;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "To get on the ship over there, you should enter the ^4d4dffShining Portal^000000.";
		mes "All transportation is done through portals.";
		setquest 7471;
		completequest 7471;
		next;
		cutin "nov_lumin01.bmp", 0;
		mes "[Lumin]";
		mes "Yes.";
		next;
		classchange HIDDEN_WARP_NPC, "", bc_self;// todo: classchange self remain on map
		cutin "fly_trock.bmp",2;
		mes "[Captain Carocc]";
		mes "Oh boy.";
		mes "What a cute reaction.";
		close2;
		cutin "",255;
		end;
	}
	cutin "nov_lumin01.bmp",0;
	mes "[Lumin]";
	mes ".....";
	next;
	select("Should I introduce myself?", "My name is ~!");
	mes "[" + strcharinfo(0) + "]";
	mes "I am " + strcharinfo(0) + "!";
	next;
	mes "[Lu]";
	mes ".....";
	next;
	mes "[Lu]";
	mes ".....";
	mes "....So?";
	next;
	classchange HIDDEN_WARP_NPC, "", bc_self;// todo: classchange self remain on map
	mes "- Lu just walked away with a cynical look on his face.";
	next;
	cutin "fly_trock.bmp",2;
	mes "[Captain Carocc]";
	mes "Looks like... he has a shy personality.";
	mes "When you get to Izlude, will you check on him?";
	next;
	mes "[Captain Carocc]";
	mes "I'll be busy sailing the ship around the island.";
	mes "Let's go, shall we?";
	close2;
	cutin "",255;
	end;

OnInit:
	questinfo 7471, QTYPE_QUEST, 1, Job_Novice;
	setquestinfo_req 7471,21008,1;
	end;
}

int_land,58,69,5	script	Sailor#intro_npc04	4W_SAILOR,{
	if (isbegin_quest(21008) == 1) {
		if (countitem(6008) < 2) {
			mes "[Sailor]";
			mes "These Porings stole materials I needed to repair the ship. Can you help me to get them back?";
			mes "There are plenty of Porings on this island.";
			next;
			mes "[Sailor]";
			mes "I would really appreciate it if you help me.";
			mes "I am not allowed to go further into the island.";
			mes "That's why I'm asking for your help~";
			close;
		}
		mes "[Sailor]";
		mes "Unbelievable, perfect! Any chance you want to join my crew?";
		mes "Enough chitchat!!";
		mes "Come on, we're ready to set sail!";
		mes "Thank you so much!";
		next;
		mes "[Sailor]";
		mes "If you want to sail with us to Izlude, jump on board through the portal!";
		delitem 6008,2;
		getexp 100,100;
		getitem 611,5;
		completequest 21008;
		next;
		mes "[Sailor]";
		mes "Oh, and take these ^4d4dffMagnifiers^000000.";
		mes "When you hunt monsters you can find ^4d4dffunidentified items^000000.";
		next;
		mes "[Sailor]";
		mes "Using a Magnifier will identify the item.";
		next;
		mes "[Sailor]";
		mes "Maybe you already have some unidentified items from your fights with the Porings?";
		close;
	}
	mes "[Sailor]";
	mes "The ship is heading to Izlude soon~!";
	mes "I'll let you know when we set sail~!";
	close;

OnInit:
	questinfo 21002, QTYPE_QUEST, 1, Job_Novice;
	setquestinfo_req 21002,21008,1;
	end;
}

izlude,198,213,3	script	Captain Carocc#iz	4_M_REINDEER,5,5,{
	cutin "fly_trock.bmp", 2;
	if (Class == Job_Novice && BaseLevel < 15) {
		if (isbegin_quest(4269) == 2) {
			if (isbegin_quest(7471) == 2 || isbegin_quest(7472) > 0) {
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Oh, "+strcharinfo(0)+"!";
				mes "At the wharf already?";
				mes "I guess you are doing well at the academy.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "I'm going to be docked and reparing the ship here for a while.";
				mes "After, I will be taking the same route I tried before.";
			} else {
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Hmm? You must be a student of the Criatura Academy.";
				mes "Were you on my ship?";
				mes "Hmm, I can't remember.";
				next;
				mes "[Carocc]";
				mes "Oh well, it happens.";
				mes "Shall I go easy on you since you are a student of the Academy?";
				mes "Though I am still the captain of the ship.";
			}
			next;
			mes "[Carocc]";
			mes "I plan on taking off as soon as the repairs are complete.";
			mes "The route will open with ^4d4dffPharos Lighthouse^000000 by then.";
		} else {
			if (isbegin_quest(7471) == 2) {
				if (!isbegin_quest(7472)) {
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "This is Izlude.";
					mes "The best city for your dreams to take flight.";
					next;
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "Although I don't know how you'll do here,";
					mes "I've seen a lot of young people like you, while operating the ship.";
					next;
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "There were those among them who succeeded and failed and went back after being unable to adjust.";
					mes "I want you to have a successful start with this place.";
					next;
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "Did you know?";
					mes "Izlude has a new institute for budding adventurers like you!";
					next;
					select("You mean the Academy?");
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "Yes! It's called the ^4d4dffRoyal Criatura Academy^000000.";
					mes "It was founded by the Rune Midgard lineage to help out new adventurers.";
					next;
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "A friend of mine works there, you should seek him out.";
					mes "He could help you out with many things.";
					next;
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "He usually talks to new adventurers near the entrance of the academy.";
					mes "Go and meet him there.";
					next;
					if (!isbegin_quest(7473)) {
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "His name is ^4d4dffHun^000000";
						mes "I will mark his spot on the map.";
						setquest 7472;
						viewpoint 1,122,207,0,0x4d4dff;
						next;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "The ^4d4dffMini map can be seen on the top-right of the screen.";
						mes "You can zoom in by clicking +, zoom out with -. The waypoints for NPCs will be marked on it. ^000000";
						next;
						cutin "tutorial02.bmp", 4;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "You received a Quest from ^4d4dffCaptain Carocc.";
						mes "The quest information can be checked from the quest window.";
						next;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "Quest window can be opened by pressing ^4d4dffAlt + U^000000 keys together.";
						next;
						cutin "", 255;
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "If you need more help with the map, click <NAVI>[Hun]<INFO>izlude,122,207</INFO></NAVI> here.";
						mes "Yes, the part that says 'Hun' on this message window.";
						next;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "^4d4dffIf you see a link like <NAVI>[Hun]<INFO>izlude,122,207</INFO></NAVI>, clicking it will give you navigation directions.";
						cutin "navi01.bmp", 4;
						next;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "^4d4dffArrows pointing to the location of the objective will pop up along with the navigation help.";
						cutin "navi02.bmp", 4;
						next;
						cutin "", 255;
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "Anyway, my friend will help you register with the academy.";
						mes "I hope it can help you out in your journey.";
						close;
					} else {
						select("I know who you're talking about.");
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "Then there's no worry.";
						mes "He'll introduce you to the academy.";
						next;
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "I will show you the direction. You can try it again.";
						mes "By the way, did I tell you his name? His name is ^4d4dffHun^000000.";
						viewpoint 1,122,207,1,0x4d4dff;
						next;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "^4d4dff Mini map can be seen on the right top of the screen.";
						mes "You can zoom in by clicking +, zoom out with -. The waypoints for NPC will be marked on it. ^000000";
						next;
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "If you need more help with the map, click <NAVI>[Hun]<INFO>izlude,122,207</INFO></NAVI> here.";
						mes "Yes, the part that says [Hun] on this message window.";
						next;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "^4d4dffIf you see a link like <NAVI>[Hun]<INFO>izlude,122,207</INFO></NAVI>,";
						mes "clicking it will give you navigation directions.";
						cutin "navi01.bmp", 4;
						next;
						mes "!- Information -!";
						mes "^4d4dffArrows pointing to the location of the objective will pop up along with navigation help";
						cutin "navi02.bmp", 4;
						next;
						cutin "", 255;
						mes "[Carocc]";
						mes "Anyway, my friend will help you register with the academy.";
						mes "I hope it will help you out in your journey.";
						close;
					}
				} else if (isbegin_quest(7472) == 1) {
					mes "[Carocc]";
					mes "If you want, you can explore the world right away.";
					mes "However, I recommend you visit the Academy first.";

				mes "Then use it next time.";

		}
	}
	close2;
	cutin "", 255;
	end;

OnInit:
	questinfo 7472, QTYPE_QUEST, 1, Job_Novice;
	setquestinfo_level 7472,1,14;

	end;

// - Airship Sign
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

	.@total = isbegin_quest(7475) + isbegin_quest(7476) + isbegin_quest(7477);

		if (!isbegin_quest(7475)) {
			mes "==== Airship Information====";

// - Therapist (Red Herb Quest + First Aid)
// - Gives the player a basic quest and teaches them First Aid.
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
iz_ac01,59,43,3	script	Therapist#ac	4_M_6THPRIN1,{
	if (!checkweight(1304,3)) {
		mes "Quest cannot be continued due to the overfilled inventory.";
		mes "Please try it again after organizing the items.";
		close;
	}
	mes "[Therapist]";
	if (isbegin_quest(4269) == 2) {
		mes "Are you a student?";
		mes "Is something wrong?";
		next;
		.@menu$ = "Help me!:Teach me the First Aid skill:^ff0000Red Herb Quest^000000:Save Location";
	} else {
		mes "This is the dispensary of the Royal Criatura Academy.";
		mes "How can I help you?";
		next;
		.@menu$ = "Help me!:First Aid Skill::I want to rest.";
	}
	switch(select(.@menu$)) {
	case 1:
		if (BaseLevel <= 20) {
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "Are you injured?";
			mes "Even the emergency treatment didn't work for you?";
			next;
			npcskill "AL_HEAL", 3, 50, 60;
			percentheal 0,50;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "Is that good enough?";
			mes "Have you recovered?";
			mes "If you have any sense, get some rest before you go back out.";
			close;
		} else {
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "I feel sorry for you but...";
			mes "I can only give my free healing service to those under base level 20.";
			mes "You don't look like you're going to die anyways.";
			next;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "Just take a rest here until you've recovered.";
			mes "There are lots of vacant beds!";
			close;
		}
		break;
	case 2:
		if (getskilllv("NV_FIRSTAID")) {
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "You already know about First Aid.";
			mes "There's too much work to do. Don't bother me.";
			close;
		} else {
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "How commendable!";
			mes "First Aid is a skill that transfers SP to HP during emergency situations.";
			next;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "The recovery ratio is very minimal...";
			mes "It can help you avoid dying but it won't give you much HP.";
			specialeffect2 EF_BEGINSPELL6;
			specialeffect2 EF_SPELLBREAKER;
			next;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "Press ^4d4dffALT + S^000000 to open your Skill window and see your skills.";
			skill "NV_FIRSTAID", 1, 0;
			skill_nov = 3;
			getexp 1000,40;
			next;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "If you press ^4d4dffF12^000000...";
			mes "The shortcut window will open up with nine small compartments to register your skills to.";
			next;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "Dragging the right hand corner on the shortcut window, you can expand more skill shortcut lines.";
			next;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "It's simple to use.. ^4d4dffEach slot responds to individual keys from F1 to F9^000000.";
			mes "Needed skills or items can be quickly accessed after using the shortcuts.";
			next;
			cutin "tutorial05.bmp", 4;
			mes "!- Information -!";
			mes "You can register needed items or skills to ^4d4dffshortcut slots by dragging the icons to the slot.";
			next;
			mes "!- Information -!";
			mes "^4d4dff The registered items and equipment at^4d4dff the slots can be immediately used or armed by pressing the correponding F1 - F9 keys.";
			next;
			mes "!- Information -!";
			mes "After setting the ^4d4dffshortcut keys as you want, you can use the corresponding shortcut key.";
			next;
			mes "!- Information -!";
			mes "^4d4dffYou should register your most frequently used items and skills, to access them at your convenience.";
			cutin "", 255;
			next;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "Now open the skill window and register [First Aid] as shortcut key, then use it.";
			mes "You will find it is more covenient to use this way.";
			close;
		}
	case 3:
		if (!isbegin_quest(7478)) {
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "Have you investigated the growing plants in the field?";
			mes "^4d4dff Red Plant, Blue Plant, Green Plant, White Plant^000000etc..";
			next;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "You can get different colored herbs from the various plants.";
			mes "Processing herbs can turn them into various useful potions.";
			next;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "Now, shall we collect the Red Herb by hand?";
			next;
			mes "[Therapist]";
			mes "There should be a ^4d4dffRed Plant growing near the academy building.^000000.";
			mes "I secretly planted it for today.";
			mes "Go and get the ^4d4dff1 Red Herb^000000.";
			setquest 7478;
			close;
		} else if (isbegin_quest(7478) == 1) {
			if (countitem(507) > 0) {
				mes "[Therapist]";
				mes "You got it.";
				mes "^4d4dffYou could eat this herb and get the benefit of it immediately, but it will be more potent if you make it into a potion.^000000.";

	case 4:

// - Cultivated Red Plant (Red Herb Quest)
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
izlude,141,251,0	script	Cultivated Red Plant#0	1078,3,3,{
	end;

OnTouch:
	if (isbegin_quest(7478) == 1 && !isbegin_quest(7479)) {
		specialeffect EF_STEAL;
		emotion ET_SMILE, getnpcid(0, "Academy Student#"+strnpcinfo(2));
		emotion ET_SURPRISE, playerattached();
		donpcevent "Cultivated Red Plant#"+strnpcinfo(2)+"::OnDisable";
	}
	end;

OnDisable:
	disablenpc "Cultivated Red Plant#"+strnpcinfo(2);
	initnpctimer;
	end;

OnTimer30000:
	enablenpc "Cultivated Red Plant#"+strnpcinfo(2);
	stopnpctimer;
	end;
}

		if (select("What are you talking about?", "Who're you?") == 1) {
			mes "[Lumin]";

	end;

	setquestinfo_req 7479,7478,1;

// - Trainer Mainz
// - Teaches the player about Status Effects (poison, stun, etc).
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
iz_ac01,134,47,5	script	Trainer Mainz#ac	4_M_KY_KNT,4,4,{
	if (!isbegin_quest(4269)) {
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "Ah ha....";
		mes "What should I do with this lunchbox?";
		close;
	}
	if (isbegin_quest(15000) == 1) {
		if (!checkweight(1201,1) || (MaxWeight - Weight) < 40) {
			mes "- Here, just a moment!! -";
			mes "- As you are overloaded with too many items in your inventory -";
			mes "- You can't receive the items anymore -";
			mes "- Let yourself be lightened up -";
			mes "- and please try again -";
			close;
		}
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "Are you ready to learn about abnormal statuses? I promise that I won't trick you anymore. I am a ''trainer'' after all, right?";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "First of all, I'll tell you about <^FF0000Poison^000000>.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "As you already experienced, when you are poisoned, your body turns purple and you lose a little HP every second.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "You can't lose HP forever, so you won't actually die from poison.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "Experiencing is believing! I will put you in a poisoned status.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "Observe what happens to you while poisoned.";
		next;
		sc_start SC_POISON, 30000, 0;
		mes "You are- <^FF0000Poisoned^000000>.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "......";
		next;
		sc_end SC_POISON;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "Do you understand poisoned status better now? After a time you'll be detoxed naturally, but if you're being attacked, it's dangerous to wait on being detoxed naturally.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "This is where detoxicants such as <^0022FFGreen Herb^000000>, <^0022FFGreen Potion^000000>, <^0022FFPanacea^000000> and <^0022FFRoyal Jelly^000000> come in handy.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "Next, I'll tell you about<^FF0000 Stun^000000.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "While you are Stunned, stars will circle around your head and you won't be able to move. Basically, you'll be ''defenseless''.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "While defenseless, you can't move, use skills, or use items.";
		mes "So, it is impossible to recover from it by yourself.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "The exception is you can recover from Stun with a skill called <^0022FFGentle Touch-Cure^000000>, if your job class is Sura.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "You can also recover with skills such as the a Priest's <^0022FFRecovery ^000000> or Arch Bishop's <^0022FFLauda Ramus^000000>, if one is around.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "Let me show you what happens with the Stun status in practice!";
		next;
		sc_start SC_STUN, 30000, 0;
		mes "<^FF0000 Stun ^000000>.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "......";
		next;
		sc_end SC_STUN;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "How was it?";
		mes "Didn't you feel helpless since you couldn't move?";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "Imagine that you are in that status while monsters are rushing your way...";
		mes "Believe me, it'll happen.";
		emotion ET_KEK;
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "Next up, I will teach you about <^FF0000Sleep^000000>.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "In Sleep status, you fall asleep with a <Zzz> message over your head.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "Same as the Stun status you are defenseless, but the difference is you recover from an enemy's attack.";
		next;
		mes "[Mainz]";
		mes "However in Sleep status, the possibility of being hit by ''Critical'' attacks from enemy attack is increased, so you are in danger and exposed to severe damage.";

// - Odd Novice
// - Introduces the player to the concept of Super Novices.
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
iz_ac01,36,52,3	script	Odd Novice#ac	4_M_SIT_NOVICE,{
	mes "[Odd Novice]";
	mes "Ahaaa~~ here at the dispensary.";
	mes "Playing hooky is cool and awesome.";
	if (Class == Job_Novice) {
		mes "A novice, but what are you?";
		mes "Are you the same kind of novice?";
		next;
		.@choice = rand(1,10);
		if (.@choice < 3) {
			mes "[Odd Novice]";
			mes "Hmmm... you look like you have some talent.";
			mes "Being in a good mood, shall I show you this newfangled thing?";
			next;
			.@message = select("Newfangled?", "Who are you..?", "Why are you here?", "End Conversation");
		} else {
			.@message = select("Who are you..?", "Why are you here?", "End Conversation") +1;
		}
		switch(.@message)
		{
		case 1:
			mes "[Odd Novice]";
			mes "I may look ordinary to you but I have a newfangled talent.";
			mes "Not my fault if you are shocked when you see it.";
			next;
			mes "[Odd Novice]";
			mes "OK. Where should I start?";
			mes "First, Bash!";
			specialeffect2 EF_BASH;
			next;
			mes "[Odd Novice]";
			mes "Hehehe.. Surprised?";
			mes "I'm just pretending...";
			mes "It's not a real punch.";
			next;
			mes "[Odd Novice]";
			mes "Looks like you were surprised!";
			specialeffect2 EF_BLESSING;
			next;
			mes "[Odd Novice]";
			mes "Just keep calm,";
			mes "and have a potion.";
			mes "But that's not the last of it.";
			specialeffect2 EF_STEAL;
			next;
			mes "[Odd Novice]";
			mes "I have stolen one thread of your hair!";
			mes "Good thing I don't believe in Voodooism.";
			mes "Count yourself lucky.";
			next;
			mes "[Odd Novice]";
			mes "The last one is a doozey, to say the least!";
			mes "Shall I? it's newfangled, I tell ya.";
			mes "Hmm, idling away too long,";
			mes "Coulda used all the skills by now.";
			specialeffect EF_SIGHT, AREA, "Odd Novice#nk1";
			next;
			mes "[Odd Novice]";
			mes "Ugh, all my SP is gone...";
			mes "such a waste... I am tired.";
			mes "I am gonna head back to rest.";
			mes "So long, bye-bye~~ Don't bother me anymore.";
			close;
		case 2:
			if (.@choice == 10) {
				mes "[Odd Novice]";
				mes "What? You're disturbing me.";
				mes "Get away from me kid, you're botherin' me.";
				close;
			} else {
				switch(rand(1,3)) {
					case 1:
						mes "[Odd Novice]";
						mes "Me? I'm Novice.";
						mes "What? Strange? You seein' me for the first time?";
						next;
						mes "[Odd Novice]";
						mes "If I look shabby to you, you should go find a mirror.";
						mes "You and I are wearing the same thing, pal.";
						close;
					case 2:
						mes "[Odd Novice]";
						mes "I'm what you call a Novice of all Novices.";
						mes "A Jack of all trades, but a master of none.";
						next;
						mes "[Odd Novice]";
						mes "If you don't graduate from school, hang around, and only mimic the lifestyle of others, you'll end up like me.";
						next;
						mes "[Odd Novice]";
						mes "There's a paper thin difference between genius and idiot.";
						mes "Those of versatility but of no specialty, that is the Super Novice.";
						mes "That's what everyone calls us.";
						close;
					case 3:
						mes "[Odd Novice]";
						mes "A rose by any other name, as they say...";
						mes "I am what I am. A Super Novice!";
						close;
				}
			}
		case 3:
			if (.@choice == 10) {
				mes "[Odd Novice]";
				mes "What? You're disturbing me.";
				mes "Get away from me kid, you're botherin' me.";
				close;
			} else {
				if (!callfunc("F_CanChangeJob")) {
					mes "[Odd Novice]";
					mes "Hanging here talking like this, why don't you go and change your job already instead of sticking around?";
					mes "Hmm did you want to be like me, maybe?";
					next;

					close;
				} else {
					switch(rand(1,3)) {
					case 1:

						mes "Hmmm. Dirty mouth!";
						mes "When I was at your age,";
						mes "if I recklessly spoke like you, I was dragged to the backside mountain, and then...";
						next;
						mes "[Odd Novice]";
						mes "OK... that's enough..";
						mes "When I'm in a good mood?";
						mes "I am using good words now,";
						mes "so go away silently, yes?";
						close;
					case 2:
						mes "[Odd Novice]";

						mes "I don't need to tell you.";

						mes "Scary, isn't it?";

		case 4:

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

	if (!checkweight(1301,3)) {
		mes "- Quest cannot be continued due to your overfilled inventory. -";
		close;
	}

	if (Class == Job_Novice) {
		if (!isbegin_quest(1237)) {
			mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
			mes "How are you doing with your basic studies?";
			mes "You should hear some information about shops.";
			next;
			if (select("I'm doing fine by myself!", "Ok I'll listen!") == 1) {
				mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
				mes "If you listen carefully, I will give you a souvenir.";
				close;
			}
			mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
			mes "Wise choice.";
			mes "Rune Midgard has many shops and some varieties of currencies.";
			mes "So you need to listen to me well to understand how use them accordingly.";
			setquest 1237;
			close;
		}
		if (!isbegin_quest(1238)) {
			mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
			mes "Let's start.";
		} else if (isbegin_quest(1238) == 1) {
			if (countitem(501) > 0) {
				mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
				mes "Ok, here's 1 ^0000ffRed Potion^000000.";
				mes "You can use this on a field or in a dungeon.";
				mes "As a reward, I'll give you a couple of ^ff0000Fly Wing^000000s as well.";
				completequest 1238;
				setquest 1239;
				getitem 12323,50;// N_Fly_Wing
				getexp 1300,100;
				close;
			}
			mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
			mes "Go to the shop, buy one ^0000ffRed Potion^000000, and bring it back.";
			mes "You have that much money, right?";
			next;
			mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
			mes "If not, go hunt monsters in the vicnity and then when you sell their loot, you should make enough money.";
			next;
			if (select("I will do it.", "Question about the shop.") == 1) {
				mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
				mes "When you return we can move on to the next lesson.";
				mes "Hurry back.";
				close;
			}
			mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
		} else {
			if (!isbegin_quest(1240)) {
				mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
				mes "On to the next lesson.";
				mes "In your future travels,";
				mes "you will acquire many items in your inventory.";
				next;
				mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
				mes "Among those items, there will be ones that you can't drop or trade... these are for quests. All items are important sometimes you will also find them to be a burden.";

				mes "When that happens, sell what you can to shops in order to decrease your inventory.";
				mes "I'll give you an example.";
				mes "Go to a shop to unload this.";
				next;
				switch(select("I don't want to do it.", "I will do it.", "Question about the shop.")) {
					case 1:
						mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
						mes "Stingy person!";
						close;

				next;
				mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";
				break;
			case 2:
				mes "[Shop Helper Leonie]";

				next;

// - Attribute Expert
// - Teaches the player about Attributes.
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
iz_ac01,53,74,3	script	Attribute Expert#ac	1_M_WIZARD,{
	mes "[Attribute Expert]";
	mes "Are you a new student? Ask me anything if you have questions about atttributes. I am an attribute expert.";
	next;
	while(1) {
		switch(select("What are attributes?", "Harmony of attributes", "Experience of attributes", "End Conversation")) {
		case 1:
			mes "[Attribute Expert]";
			mes "All materials in the world have their own attributes.";
			next;
			mes "[Attribute Expert]";
			mes "There are many types of attributes. There are 4 elemental attributes... ^0D6EF2Water^000000, ^006600Wind^000000, ^FF0000Fire^000000, ^B97246Earth^000000.";
			next;
			mes "[Attribute Expert]";
			mes "There are also more uncommon ones like... Neutral, Poison, Holy, Dark, Angel, Undead.";
			mes "There are more types than you would think, right?";
			next;
			mes "[Attribute Expert]";
			mes "All right, here's the question. Which attribute do we belong to?";
			next;
			if (select("Water", "Wind", "Fire", "Earth", "Neutral", "Poison", "Holy", "Dark", "Angel", "Undead") == 5) {
				mes "[Attribute Expert]";
				mes "Correct! You are good. Yes we belong to the Neutral attribute.";
				next;
				break;
			} else {
				mes "[Attribute Expert]";
				mes "Is that what you think?";
				mes "Actually, we belong to the Neutral attribute.";
				next;
				break;
			}
			next;
			mes "[Attribute Expert]";
			mes "Then, why do we need attributes? Maybe you know the answer... right?";
			next;
			break;
		case 2:
			mes "[Attribute Expert]";
			mes "Everything needs to balance with something srong and something weak. So ^3131FFbalance and harmony^000000 comes can always be achieved.";
			next;
			mes "[Attribute Expert]";
			mes "Balance and harmony are strongly related to your power, too. So pay attention.";
			next;
			while(1) {
				switch(select("Water", "Fire", "Earth", "Wind", "Etc...", "I already know")) {
				case 1:
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "^0D6EF2Water^000000 is stronger than ^FF0000Fire^000000, so Water gives bonus damage to anything with Fire attribute!";
					mes "But it is weak to ^006600Wind^000000.";
					next;
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "Examples of monsters with the Water Attribute are Poring and Roda Frog... have you heard of them?";
					next;
					continue;
				case 2:
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "^FF0000Fire^000000 is stronger than ^B97246Earth^000000, so Water gives bonus damage to anything with Earth attribute!";
					mes "Examples of monsters with the Fire Attribute are Drops and Picky.";
					next;
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "Examples of monsters with the Fire Attribute are Drops and Picky.";
					next;
					continue;
				case 3:
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "^B97246Earth^000000 is stronger than ^006600Wind^000000, so Earth gives bonus damage to anything with Wind attribute!";
					mes "But it is weak to ^FF0000Fire^000000.";
					next;
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "Examples of monsters with the Earth Attribute are Pupa and Fabre.";
					next;
					continue;
				case 4:
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "^006600Wind^000000 is stronger than ^0D6EF2Water^000000, so Wind gives bonus damage to anything with Water attribute!";
					mes "But it is weak to ^B97246Earth^000000.";
					next;
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "Examples of monsters with the Wind Attribute are ChonChon and Hornet.";
					next;
					continue;
				case 5:
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "^3131FFPoison^000000 is stronger than Fire, Wind, and Earth, but it is weak to the Undead attribute.";
					next;
					continue;
				case 6:
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "Super important to know.. isn't it?";
					next;
					break;
				}
				break;
			}
			break;
		case 3:
			if (!isbegin_quest(2299)) {
				mes "[Attribute Expert]";
				mes "Do you want to experience an attribute?";
				next;
				mes "[Attribute Expert]";
				mes "All right, do you see those ^3131FFFire Eggs^000000 over there?";
				mes "Go over there and smack one of them.";
				mes "Don't worry about destroying it.";
				setquest 2299;
				close;
			} else if (isbegin_quest(2299) == 1) {
				mes "[Attribute Expert]";
				mes "How is it? Have you ever attacked Fire Eggs before?";
				next;
				switch(select("Yes", "No", "I want to quit.")) {
				case 1:
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "How much damage did you give?";
					next;
					input .@input, 1, 100000;
					if (.@input < 10) {
						mes "[Attribute Expert]";
						mes "Oh man, "+.@input+"! Are you even trying?";
						mes "You're barely hitting it.";
						next;
					} else if (.@input > 9 && .@input < 100001) {
						mes "[Attribute Expert]";
						mes "You're good I guess...";
						next;
					} else {
						mes "[Attribute Expert]";
						mes "But wait, that's impossible.";
						close;
					}
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "All right. Lesson over.";
					next;
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "I am not sure if you remember, monsters with ^FF0000Fire^000000 are weak against ^0D6EF2Water^000000.";
					next;
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "I will inbue you the ^0D6EF2Water^000000 attribute temporarily.";
					mes "If you attack the Fire Eggs again you should do more damage now.";
					next;
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "This is the last chance!";
					mes "Hurry up, the attribute magic will be gone if you take too much time.";
					completequest 2299;
					// ConsumeSpecialItem 12115
					if (Class == Job_Novice)
						getexp 100,20;
					close;
				case 2:
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "Go and smack those eggs over there.";
					mes "The egg of an ant is strong, so don't worry too much about destroying them.";
					close;
				case 3:
					mes "[Attribute Expert]";
					mes "There is nothing I can do. But I will help you if you need anything else.";
					erasequest 2299;
					close;
				}
			} else {
				mes "[Attribute Expert]";
				mes "Magic basically consists of different attribute attacks. You can also give attributes to your weapon by using a skill or item. You will learn more the longer you play. Good luck!";
				close;
			}
			break;
		case 4:
			mes "[Attribute Expert]";
			mes "Are you interested in the depth of different attributes yet?";
			close;
		}
	}

OnInit:
	questinfo 2299, QTYPE_QUEST, 0;
	end;
}

// - General Store Owner
// - Sells the player the Novice Combination Book and Kit.
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
iz_ac01,68,49,3	script	General Store Owner#ac	4_F_03,{
	if (!checkweight(1304,3)) {
		mes "Quest cannot be continued due to the overfilled inventory.";
		mes "Please try it again after organizing the items.";
		close;
	}
	mes "[Querrie]";
	mes "Are you interested in the beginner's guild?";
	mes "I am selling Combination books and kits.";
	next;
	mes "[Querrie]";
	mes "For the Criatura students below level 20, a special sale is going on. Hope you to buy a lot!!!";
	next;
	switch(select("Novice Combination Book", "Combination Kit", "Cancel.")) {
	case 1:
		if (isbegin_quest(4269) && isbegin_quest(7478)) {
			mes "[Querrie]";
			mes "Have you been treated by the Therapist?";
			mes "At the medical botany class, you may receive a guild book.";
			next;
			if (select("Ah... is that so?", "I lost it.") == 1) {
				mes "[Querrie]";
				mes "Come back later to buy a lot of the guild combination kits~~~";
				mes "I am selling them at a jaw dropping price to students below base level 20.";
				close;
			}
			mes "[Querrie]";
			mes "Say what?";
		} else {
			mes "[Querrie]";
			mes "You mean the combination book.";
		}
		mes "A book costs you 1000z.";
		next;
		if (select("Buy", "Don't buy.") == 2) {
			mes "[Querrie]";
			mes "You can get one next time.";
		} else {
			if (Zeny >= 1000) {
				mes "[Querrie]";
				mes "Here you are.";
				mes "This book is for beginners. But it will allow you combine useful tools together, if you use it correctly.";
				Zeny -= 1000;
				getitem 11058,1;// Novice_Combi_Book
			} else {
				mes "[Querrie]";
				mes "The book price is 1000 zeny.";
				mes "You seem to be short on zeny.";
			}
		}
		close;
	case 2:
		if (BaseLevel <= 20) {
			mes "[Querrie]";
			mes "Breaking news! Special sale for you only!";
			mes "One combination kit for only 30z!";
			mes "How many do you need?";
		} else {
			mes "[Querrie]";
			mes "No sales today, but fair prices.";
			mes "One combination kit costs you 500z.";
			mes "How many pieces do you need?";
		}
		next;
		input .@input;
		if (!.@input) {
			mes "[Querrie]";
			mes "Well, you don't need to buy one now.";
			mes "Come back and get one next time.";
			close;
		}
		if (.@input > 99) {
			mes "[Querrie]";
			mes "How many pieces do you need?";
			mes "You can buy up to 99 at once.";
			close;
		}
		set .@cost, .@input * (BaseLevel <= 20 ? 30 : 500);
		mes "[Querrie]";
		mes .@input+" combination kits will cost you "+.@cost+".... zeny.";
		if (Zeny < .@cost) {
			mes "You look short of money for that amount.";
			close;
		}
		mes "Thank you. Come back again.";
		Zeny -= .@cost;
		getitem 12849,.@input;// Combination_Kit
		close;
	case 3:
		close;
	}
}

// - Battle Instructor
// - Gives the player monster hunting quests.
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
iz_ac01,59,83,3	script	Battle Instructor#08	4_M_NOV_HUNT,{
	if (!checkweight(1201,1) || (MaxWeight - Weight) < 2000) {
		mes "- You have too many items.";
		mes "- Clear inventory and try again.";
		close;
	}
	if (Class == Job_Novice) {
		if (isbegin_quest(4269) == 2) {
			if (JobLevel == 10) {
				mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
				mes "You shouldn't still be novice, you are high enough to change your job.";
				mes "But I won't stop you, even if you stay like this...";
				next;
				mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
				mes "Try talking to to ^ff0000each job instructor^000000 on the 2nd floor of the Academy if you aren't sure what job you want yet.";
				for (set .@i,0; .@i < 6; set .@i,.@i+1) {
					set .@quest_id,11339+.@i;
					setarray .@bexp[0],90,90,135,200,0,120;
					setarray .@jexp[0],50,50,100,175,0,90;
					setarray .@material[0],909,515,914,939,0,915;
					setarray .@count[0],5,1,3,3,0,2;

					if (.@quest_id == 11343)
						continue;
					if (checkquest(.@quest_id,HUNTING) == 1)
						erasequest .@quest_id;
					else if (checkquest(.@quest_id,HUNTING) == 2) {
						erasequest .@quest_id;
						if (countitem(.@material[.@i]) >= .@count[i]) {
							delitem .@material[.@i],.@count[.@i];
							getexp .@bexp[.@i],.@jexp[.@i];
							getitem 7059,1;// Cargo_Free_Ticket
						}
					}
				}
				close;
			}
			mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
			mes "Welcome!";
			mes "I am ^ff0000Battle Instructor Subino^000000.";
			mes "I ^ff0000offer simple challenges^000000 to help you to grow to be as good a soldier as fast as possible, so please, take a look...";
			next;
			switch(select("Check requests", "Warp me to the Field", "End Conversation")) {
				case 1:
					switch(select("The most delicious in the world (1~3):Carrots are delicious (1~3):Fabre rolling clothes (4~6):Barrier!! (4~6):"+(BaseLevel<7?"":"Buzzing~ (7~10)")+":Stop.")) {
						case 1:
							if (!isbegin_quest(11338)) {
								setquest 11338;
								completequest 11338;
							}
							if (checkquest(11339,HUNTING) < 2) {
								mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
								mes "^ff0000Poring^000000s are very cute monsters when you see them.";
								next;
								mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
								mes "They drop Jellopy, which are regarded as a important cooking materials in Criatura Academy, so we always need to hunt Porings.";
								next;
							}
							callsub L_Quest,11339,90,50,909,5,"Poring","can easily be found","Hunt","Jellopies";
						case 2:
							if (!isbegin_quest(11338)) {
								setquest 11338;
								completequest 11338;
							}
							if (checkquest(11340,HUNTING) < 2) {
								mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
								mes "^ff0000Lunatic^000000s are very cute animal that live near Prontera.";
								mes "Tender...soft...very cute... They are very cute........";
								next;
								mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";

								next;

								mes "Carrots lots of fibrous cells and contains vitamin A and carotin, so they are good for eyes!";
								next;
							}
							callsub L_Quest,11340,90,50,515,1,"Lunatic","is easily found","Catch","Carrot";
						case 3:

								setquest 11338;

							}
							if (checkquest(11341,HUNTING) < 2) {

		next;
		mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
		mes "It is ^ff0000displayed in the map on the top right of screen^000000.";
		mes "If you are unable to find it, you can get a help from a ^ff0000Town Guide^000000.";
		close;
	}

L_Quest:
	.@quest_id = getarg(0);
	if (checkquest(.@quest_id,HUNTING) == -1) {
		if (select("Take quest.", "Stop.") == 2) {
			mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
			mes "You don't seem to be interested.";
			mes "Come back again if you change your mind.";
			close;
		}
		mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
		if (.@quest_id == 11342) {
			mes getarg(5)+"s "+getarg(6)+" in ^ff0000West field of Prontera^000000.";
			mes getarg(5)+"s are difficult to catch for a Novice... but if you gather more Novices, you can do it.";
			next;
			mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
		} else
			mes getarg(5)+" "+getarg(6)+" at the ^ff0000West field of Izlude^000000.";
		mes getarg(7)+" ^ff0000"+(.@quest_id==11344?"5":"10")+" "+getarg(5)+"s^000000 and bring ^ff0000"+getarg(4)+" "+getarg(8)+"^000000.";
		mes "You can check received quests by pressing ^ff0000Alt + U^000000.";
		setquest .@quest_id;
		close;
	} else if (checkquest(.@quest_id,HUNTING) == 1) {
		if (select("End Conversation", "Give up on the quest.") == 2) {
			mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
			mes "Will you really give up on the quest?";
			next;
			if (select("End Conversation", "Give up for sure.") == 2) {
				mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
				mes "You can try the quest again for as long as you need my help, so come back anytime.";
				erasequest .@quest_id;
			}
		}
		close;
	} else {
		if (countitem(getarg(3)) < getarg(4)) {
			mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
			mes "You don't have enough ^ff0000"+getarg(8)+"^000000.";
			mes "Do better!";
			next;
			if (select("End Conversation", "Give up on the quest.") == 2) {
				mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
				mes "Will you really give up on the quest?";
				next;
				if (select("End Conversation", "Yes, give up.") == 2) {
					mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
					mes "You can try the quest again for as long as you need my help, so come back anytime.";
					erasequest .@quest_id;
				}
			}
			close;
		}
		mes "[Battle Instructor Subino]";
		mes "Wow..!!";
		mes "Well done!!";
		erasequest .@quest_id;
		delitem getarg(3), getarg(4);
		getexp getarg(1), getarg(2);
		getitem 7059,1;// Cargo_Free_Ticket
		close;
	}

OnInit:
	questinfo 11339, QTYPE_QUEST ,0 ,Job_Novice;
	questinfo 11340, QTYPE_QUEST ,0 ,Job_Novice;
	questinfo 11341, QTYPE_QUEST ,0 ,Job_Novice;
	questinfo 11342, QTYPE_QUEST ,0 ,Job_Novice;
	questinfo 11344, QTYPE_QUEST ,0 ,Job_Novice;
	setquestinfo_req 11339,4269,2;
	setquestinfo_req 11340,4269,2;
	setquestinfo_req 11341,4269,2;
	setquestinfo_req 11342,4269,2;
	setquestinfo_req 11344,4269,2;
	end;
}

iz_ac01,95,46,5	script	Kafra Guide Trainer#ac	4_F_KAFRA1,{
	cutin "kafra_01.bmp", 2;
	if (isbegin_quest(4269) == 2) {
		mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
		mes "Welcome! Kafra service is always close to your heart.";
		next;
		mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
		mes "For those who are using the Kafra service for the first time,";
		mes "Kafra service offers a thorough information rundown~!";
		while(1) {
			next;
			mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
			mes "Tell us what you would like to know";
			mes "about the Kafra service~!";
			next;
			switch(select("Saving", "Storage Service", "Teleport Service", "Use of Pushcart Service", "Check Other Information", "Cancel")) {
			case 1:
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Save service is for when you ^8B4513die in battle^000000 or use an item like ^8B4513Butterfly Wings^000000. You will be sent back to your Save Location.";
				next;
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Easy to understand~?";
				mes "You want to try the Save service~?";
				next;
				if (select("No", "Yes") == 1) {
					mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
					mes "Don't be afraid of it~!";
					mes "Save service doesn't swallow you.";
					mes "If you change your mind, you can definitely come back and try~!";
				} else {
					mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
					mes "Well~ then, for now, ^8B4513Izlude Square^000000 where the Criatura Academy is located will be saved as your save point~!.";
					next;
					mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
					mes "Voila~!";
					next;
					mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
					mes "It's already done. Easy huh?";
					savepoint "izlude",128,98,1,1;
					next;
					mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
					mes "Now, when you use a ^006400Butterfly Wing^000000, it will send you to the last saved location.";
				}
				break;
			case 2:
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Storage service is a place where you can safely store your items.";
				mes "Stored items can be accessed by all characters in your account.";
				next;
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "To use storage, you need to be Novice Job Level 6 or higher.";
				next;
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "For a small fee, most Kafra Employees will let you open your storage.";
				mes "You can even buy Kafra Cards from the Item Mall and use them to open storage from anywhere!";
				mes "Do you want to try using storage?";
				next;
				if (select("No", "Yes") == 1) {
					mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
					mes "Storage is necessary for you to survive, so use it regularly.";
				} else {
					if (!callfunc("F_CanOpenStorage")) {
						mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
						mes "To use storage, you need to be beginner level 6 or higher.";
					} else if (countitem(7059) || Zeny >= 500) {
						if (countitem(7059)) {
							delitem 7059,1;// Cargo_Free_Ticket
						} else {
							Zeny -= 500;
							RESRVPTS += 5;
						}
						mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
						mes "I'll open the storage~.";
						mes "Thanks for using our service~!";
						close2;
						cutin "", 255;
						openstorage;
						end;
					} else {
						mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
						mes "Dear customer, you don't have enough money~!";
						mes "You need 500 zeny to use storage~!";
					}
				}
				break;
			case 3:
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Teleport service is a service that sends you to various locations throughout Rune Midgard.";
				next;
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Different Kafra Employees have different teleport locations they can send you to, so you need to talk to them to find out where they're teleporting to.";
				next;
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Ok, so for educational purposes I'm offering a free teleport service here at the Academy.";
				mes "Why don't you try it out?~!";
				next;
				if (select("No", "Yes") == 1) {
					mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
					mes "You afraid of having your cells spliced or something? Don't worry, this is perfectly safe~!";
					mes "This is an essential service~";
					mes "So it's better to get used to it, ok?";
					break;
				} else {
					switch(select("Academy 1st floor Great Hall", "Academy 2nd floor Principal's Office", "Izlude southern entrance", "Use later")) {
					case 1:
						cutin "", 255;
						warp "iz_ac01", 97, 86;
						end;
					case 2:
						cutin "", 255;
						warp "iz_ac02", 101, 36;
						end;
					case 3:
						mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
						mes "This will take you to the outside of the Criatura Academy, is that ok?";
						mes "If you want to come back to the academy, find the entrance to the north of Izlude.";
						next;
						if (select("No", "Yes") == 1) {
							mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
							mes "You afraid of having your cells spliced or something? Don't worry, this is perfectly safe~!";
							break;
						} else {
							cutin "", 255;
							warp "izlude", 128, 98;
							end;
						}
						break;
					case 4:
						mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
						mes "You afraid of having your cells spliced or something? Don't worry, this is perfectly safe~!";
						break;
					}
				}
				break;
			case 4:
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Pushcart service is used for those who have the job ^8B4513Merchant^000000.";
				mes "To rent a Pushcart, Merchants pay a small zeny fee and that's it.";
				next;
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "If you aren't a Merchant class or if you haven't learned the Cart skill, then you can't use this Kafra service.";
				break;
			case 5:
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Among the other services we provide, there is a Customer point service system from Kafra!";
				next;
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Every time you use a Kafra Service, you get Special Reserve Points~";
				mes "You can use these points at the Kafra Headquarters in Aldebaran to trade for certain items.";
				next;
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Here, I'll show you how many Special Reserve Points you currently have.";
				next;
				if (select("Check Special Reserve Points.", "Cancel") == 2) {
					mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";

					mes "That way you can check your accumulated customer points~!";
				} else {
					mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";

					next;
					mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";

					mes "Special Reserve Points for";
					mes "rewards at the Kafra Main Office in Aldebaran. Please use our";
					mes "convenient services to see the benefits of our rewards program.";
				}
				break;
			case 6:
				mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
				mes "Kafra service is doing our best to give you the highest satisfaction that you deserve as a customer.";
				mes "Thanks for using us.";
				close2;
				cutin "", 255;
				end;
			}
		}
	} else {
		mes "[Kafra Guide Trainer]";
		mes "First, you need to complete your^8B4513 registration^000000 at the Academy's front desk.";

	if (Class == Job_Novice) {
		mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
		mes "You are t just a beginner.";
		next;

		next;
		mes "[Wedding Secretary]";

		next;
	} else {
		mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
		mes "Are you in love?";
		next;
	}
	mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
	mes "I am the Wedding Secretary sent here for those people wanting to join their lives to one another.";
	next;
	while(1) {
		mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
		mes "Please, ask about anything concerning marriage!";
		next;
		switch(select("How to get married.", "Benefits of marriage", "Adoption", "Shut up!")) {
		case 1:
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";

			next;

			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "Next, you need to prepare some tokens of appreciation. Men need a ^0000cdTuxedo^000000, Ladies need a ^0000cdWedding Dress^000000 and both need to have ^0000cdDiamond Ring^000000s as the symbol of everlasting love.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "You will also need to provide a fee of ^0000cd1 million Zeny^000000.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "Having prepared all of these things, you must create a party with just the two of you and go to the ^0000cdProntera Cathedral^000000.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "There, another  ^0000cdWedding Secretary^000000 like me is wating for you. When you speak to her, she will give more details about what to do.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "I hope that you will meet a great fiance and enjoy a happy marriage!";
			next;
			break;
		case 2:
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "To say the least, the benefit of marriage is being together forever!";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "After the wedding ceremony, you can enjoy a sweet honeymoon at the ^0000cdJawaii^000000 resort special for the happy couple.";
			next;

			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "In addition, the skill called ^0000cdRomantic Rendezvous^000000 is the most romantic one, enabling you to summon your partner to you from anywhere in the world.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "Aren't these skill great? Don't you want to get married right now?";
			next;
			break;
		case 3:
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "Being together is wonderful, but people without experience might not know the Euphoria of being a parent.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "Married couples can adopt other characters as their children.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "^0000cdHowever kids of extended jobs such as Taekwon boy/girl, Gunslinger, or Ninja can't be adopted^000000.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "And any prospecting parents need to be at least base level  ^0000cd70^000000, meaning you should be at a level responsible enough to be parents.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "Having made a family, ^0000cdaSkill to be used among the family^000000 will be earned.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "There is another skill that enables you to concrete your bond such as being able to summon your child when you miss them, or not losing your earned level if you die during battle.";
			next;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "Cute charms coming from your kid will be a bonus~";
			next;
			break;
		case 4:
			emotion ET_HUK;
			mes "[Wedding Secretary]";
			mes "Your mother didn't teach you, right?";
			mes "Mercy on you. You are ignorant of the beauty of love!!!";

// - Otter Samssoon
// - Allows the player to change their hair style and color once.

	mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
	mes "Welcome~";
	mes "I am Samssoon~! I am a royal hair designer otter sent to the Academy.";
	next;
	mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
	mes "If you take this ^ff0000Criatura Hair Coupon^000000, you change your hairstyle once for free! So do not miss this ^ff0000once in a lifetime^000000 chance~";
	next;
	switch(select("Read style book.", "Change hair style.", "How to get a coupon", "Stop.")) {
		case 1:
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "Oh my~ I am sure any hair style will suit you! You have great style~";

			input .@style;
			if (.@style > 19) {
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";

			} else if (!.@style) {
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";

					break;

					}

					if (Sex == SEX_MALE) {

					}
					break;

						mes "This style brings lucky encounters or unexpected findings while walking down the street.";
					} else {
						mes "Oh my!!? 'Hammer Fall' cut?";
						mes "Stunning hair with attraction aplenty.";
					}
					break;
				case 18:
					if (Sex == SEX_MALE) {
						mes "Oh my!!? 'Fire Pillar' cut?";
						mes "Everyone used to have this hair style.. Which means it was the trend of an era.";
					} else {
						mes "Oh my!!? 'Jupitel Thunder' cut?";
						mes "A fresh style that gives light waves from many angles.";
					}
					break;
				case 19:
					if (Sex == SEX_MALE) {
						mes "Oh my!!? 'Guillotine Fist' cut?";
						mes "It is a one-shot victory style.. just like a real man. Right?";
					} else {
						mes "Oh my!!? 'Whirlwind' cut?";
						mes "It's a cool style that flows with the wind. Lah, lah, lah, lah ~";
					}
					break;
				}
				close2;
				cutin "", 255;
				end;
			}
			close;
		case 2:
			if (!countitem(6593)) {
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Come on.. Honey~";
				mes "You should bring ^ff0000'Criatura Hair Coupon'^000000 to change your hair...";
				close;
			}
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "Honey~ What style do you want?";

			next;

			if (.@style > 19) {

				mes "Come on.. Honey~ You can use coupons for a hair style in here~";
				close;
			} else if (!.@style) {
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Oh my!!? You do not want to?";
				close;
			} else if (getlook(1) == .@style) {
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Come on, Honey~ That is the same style you have now.";
				mes "Do you want to try something new?";
				close;
			}
			callsub L_cutin, .@style;
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "Style ("+.@style+")?";
			mes "It look like this.. what do you think?";
			next;
			if (select("Good.", "No.") == 1) {
				if (!getlook(6)) {
					mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
					mes "Right!";
					mes "Honey! What about dying hair as well?";
					mes "Dying hair is also included in this service.";
					next;
					switch(select("Passionate Red:Sweet Yellow:Fatal Purple:Glamourous Orange:Comfortable Green:Clear Blue:Transparent White:Dark Black:Stop.")) {
						case 1:
							.@pallete = 8;
							break;
						case 2:
							.@pallete = 1;
							break;
						case 3:
							.@pallete = 2;
							break;
						case 4:
							.@pallete = 3;
							break;
						case 5:
							.@pallete = 4;
							break;
						case 6:
							.@pallete = 5;
							break;
						case 7:
							.@pallete = 6;
							break;
						case 8:
							.@pallete = 7;
							break;
						case 9:
							mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
							mes "No?";
							mes "Do you need more time? If you want to keep the same color, then select the one you already have.";
							close2;
							cutin "", 255;
							end;
					}
				}
				nude;
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Relax, it is almost done~";
				next;
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "- Sha sha shak shak shak -";
				mes "- Chikak, crack, crack.. -";
				mes "- Snap, snap, snap.. Crack -";
				next;
				delitem 6593,1;// Criatura_Hair_Coupon
				cutin "", 255;
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "Oh my! Oh my! Oh my!";
				mes "This hair style no.("+.@style+") suits you so welld~";
				mes "What do you think?";
				setlook 1, .@style;
				setlook 6, .@pallete;
				next;
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "I want to take care of your style always..";
				mes "But I have no choice when you go off because I belong here.";
				next;
				mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
				mes "To change hair styles, you can go to ^ff0000Alberta or Lighthalzen^000000.";
				mes "For dying hair, you can go to ^ff0000Prontera or Lighthalzen^000000.";
				close;
			}
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "Honey~ You don't like it?";
			mes "Ahem.. Do you want to read style book again?";
			mes "Take your time and tell me when you decide~ Okay?~";
			close;
		case 3:
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "You can receive a ^ff0000Criatura Hair Coupon^000000 from the ^ff0000Academy receptionist for novices at the Academy front desk or Eden Group^000000";
			next;
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "You didn't get a free coupon? Well...";
			mes "You know the equipment youd received when you arrived at Academy?";
			mes "They can trade the ^ff0000egg shell for novice^000000 to a coupon.";
			next;
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "This service has been the same since I came here. So.. no free service if you have no coupon~";
			close;
		case 4:
			mes "[Otter Samssoon]";
			mes "Oh my!!? Honey, you are not going to change hair?";
			mes "You look nice as you are now, though.";
			close;
	}

L_cutin:
	if (Sex == SEX_MALE) {
		if (getarg(0) < 10)
			cutin "hair_m_0"+getarg(0),4;
		else
			cutin "hair_m_"+getarg(0),4;
	} else {
		if (getarg(0) < 10)
			cutin "hair_f_0"+getarg(0),4;
		else
			cutin "hair_f_"+getarg(0),4;
	}
	return;
}

// - Ragie
// - Teaches the player about Transcendent and Third classes.
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
iz_ac02,149,43,3	script	Ragie#ac	1_M_BARD,{
	mes "[Ragie]";
	mes "A sudden poetic inspiration hit me!";
	next;
	mes "[Ragie]";
	mes "^3377FFBy night on Byalan Island under the moonlight, sitting alone in Izlude^000000";
	next;
	mes "[Ragie]";
	mes "^3377FFWearing Tzurugie on my belly, with deep anxiety,^000000";
	next;
	mes "[Ragie]";
	mes "^3377FFHearing I made a fortune from somewhere, killing me softly.^000000";
	next;
	mes "[Ragie]";
	mes "........";
	next;
	mes "[Ragie]";
	mes "What do you think? It's excellent, isn't it?";
	next;
	mes "[Ragie]";
	mes "I will ^FF0000transcend ^000000to ^FF00003rd job change^000000. I'll become a nice Minstrel, so I can play with a famous Wanderer like Mr. Igoo.";
	next;
	while (1) {
		switch(select("What is transcending?", "What is the 3rd job change?", "Who is Igoo?", "End Conversation")) {
		case 1:
			if (ADVJOB != 0) {
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "You seem to already know what it is!";
				next;
			} else {
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "Transcending is great. Wonderful.";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "Basically the 2nd job adventurer gets to base level 99 and job level 50, on then they can transcend.";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "Once you transcend, you go back to the base level Novice.";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "It is difficult to start as an adventure again. However, there is a merit to the hardship.";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "The most important merit is to learn new skills at a new upgraded level. In my case, I would transfer not to an ordinary Bard, but to a Minstrel.";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "But be careful, as you can only follow the path of the job you chose before transcending.";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "If you are interested in transcending, I recommend you visit the Sage castle in ^FF0000Juno^000000. I may not have reached that point myself.";
				next;
			}
			break;
		case 2:
			if (BaseLevel > 99) {
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "Oh, you know very well, don't you?";
				next;
			} else {
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "The 3rd job change is, of course, a new job.";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "Adventurers with a 2nd job can transcend to a 3rd job class once they've attained a base level of 99 and job level of 50.";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "For example, a Bard like me was an Archer in the beginning for the 1st job. Now I became a Bard, my 2nd job. As I am diligently adventuring, I may be able to change to a 3rd job.";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "Ah, of course, though I haven't transcended yet, my goal is to become a Minstrel. And I won't stop just there. Someday I will become the best Minstrel.";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "If I transcend, I would first be a Novice and then a Bard again. But someday I could be Minstrel, couldn't I?";
				next;
				mes "[Ragie]";
				mes "The choice is up to you. Be ambitious, adventurer. Someday I will sing an encouraging song for you.";
				next;
			}
			break;
		case 3:
			mes "[Ragie]";
			mes "No! You don't know the most beautiful Wanderer of this era, Igoo?";
			next;
			mes "[Ragie]";
			mes "Haven't you heard about [Volume 1 - Lost Poring] or [Volume 2 : Poring my love]?";
			next;
			mes "[Ragie]";
			mes "Then, have you never heard songs like [It's a Good day for an OCA] or [Baphomet I hardly knew you]";
			next;
			mes "[Ragie]";
			mes "All from the lovely Wanderer from Comodo, a legend at the age of 20. Not just in Rune Midgard, but wherever her wandering troupe goes, a fan club follows.";
			next;
			mes "[Ragie]";
			mes "I am ^FF0000Ragie^000000 head of the Rune Midgard branch of Igoo's informal fan club! As Igoo has gone to the 2nd world, I am taking a rest for a while. But she will be back soon.";
			next;
			mes "[Ragie]";
			mes "As I am still a lower level adventurer, I haven't followed her to the 2nd world... But you see! I will make great efforts so I can follow her everywhere one day.";
			next;
			mes "[Ragie]";
			mes "Ahaa. No sweat, no sweat. It is useless to tell such a story to those that are ignorant.";
			next;
			break;
		case 4:
			mes "[Ragie]";
			mes "Ah! I've just had another great poetic inspiration.. I must make a note.. make a note..";
			close;
		}
	}
}

//= Cream Puff
//= Gives the player a personality test to determine the class they should be.
//==============================================================================
iz_ac02,143,55,3	script	Cream Puff#ac	4_M_KID1,{
	cutin "choucream_n.bmp", 2;
	if (Class == Job_Novice) {
		emotion ET_QUESTION;
		mes "[Cream Puff]";
		mes "You are a novice, right?";
		next;
	} else {
		emotion ET_OHNO;
		mes "[Cream Puff]";
		mes "Class aptitude tests are useless for those who already have a job.";
		close2;
		cutin "", 255;
		end;
	}
	mes "[Cream Puff]";
	mes "You haven't decided your job yet?";
	next;
	if (select("No... how did you know?", "I decided.") == 2) {
		cutin "choucream_d.bmp",2;
		emotion ET_OHNO;
		mes "[Cream Puff]";
		mes "You've already decided? Ok then.";
		next;
		mes "[Cream Puff]";
		mes "I wanted you to take the Class aptitude test for fun, though...";
		close2;
		cutin "", 255;
		end;
	}
	cutin "choucream_e.bmp",2;
	emotion ET_SPARK;
	mes "[Cream Puff]";
	mes "Oh, tha's good.";
	mes "Perhaps you would be interested in the ^0000FFClass aptitude test^000000.";
	mes "I have one book left. Do you want to try? I can't guarantee it will help you decide, but at least it will be fun.";
	next;
	while(1) {
		switch(select("Class aptitude test?", "Take the Class aptitude test.", "Stop.")) {
		case 1:
			cutin "choucream_n.bmp",2;
			mes "[Cream Puff]";
			mes "The Class aptitude test is a test that recommends jobs by reviewing your personality and capability, as judged by your answers.";
			next;
			mes "[Cream Puff]";
			mes "It has 3 types of test and each one gives you 30 minutes to finish.";
			next;
			emotion ET_QUESTION;
			mes "[Cream Puff]";
			mes "If you have free time and have not decided your job... how about taking the test?";
			next;
			continue;
		case 2:
			break;
		case 3:
			cutin "choucream_d.bmp",2;
			emotion ET_HNG;
			mes "[Cream Puff]";
			mes "All right. Good bye.";
			close2;
			cutin "", 255;
			end;
		}
		break;
	}
	cutin "choucream_e.bmp",2;
	mes "[Cream Puff]";
	mes "Shall we start?";
	next;
	mes "[Cream Puff]";
	mes "The first questions are about what you would do based on a given situation.";
	next;
	mes "In the middle of the dark, you're walking in the streets of Prontera when suddenly you hear someone scream.";
	next;

		mes "- Quest can't be continued as you are overloaded with items. -";

	}

	if (Class == Job_Novice) {
		if (isbegin_quest(4269) != 2) {
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "Oh! I am sorry but in order to take this class, y'all have to register first. Ya come back here after registration at that there counter on the 1st floor, ya hear?";
			close2;
			// ConsumeSpecialItem Inspector_Certificate_
			cutin "", 255;
			end;
		}
		setarray .@manuals[0],2819,2820,2821,2822,2823,2824,2942,2941,2940;
		for (.@i = 0; .@i < 9; .@i++) {
			if (isequippedcnt(.@manuals[.@i]) || countitem(.@manuals[.@i]))
				.@has_manual = 1;
		}
		emotion ET_COOL;
		mes "[Lusa]";
		mes "Gosh darnit! You are cuter than a piglet! Are ya trying ta learn to be a ^ff0000Gunslinger^000000?";
		next;
		if (.@has_manual == 1) {
			.@menu$ = "What is a Gunslinger?:Can I try out the skills?:Becoming a Gunslinger:How can I try out the skills?:Cancel";
		} else {
			.@menu$ = "What is a Gunslinger?:Can I try out the skills?:Becoming a Gunslinger::Cancel";
		}
		switch(select(.@menu$)) {
		case 1:
			emotion ET_THROB;
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "You're so cute! A ^ff0000Gunslinger^000000 has true grit and wields their weapons to bring justice in these wild times.";
			next;
			mes "[Lusa]";
			if (Sex == SEX_MALE)
				mes "Ya know you remind me of my little brother, that varmint couldn't shoot the broadside of a barn.. at least not until I taught him.";
			else
				mes "Ya know you remind me of my little sister, that scamp couldn't shoot the broadside of barn.. at least not until I taught her.";
			next;
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "Now y'all need to understand, guns aren't some little thing that you just swing at an animal. You don't wiggle those there fingers and shock them to death.";
			next;
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "No! You shoot things, which means ya need to aim straight. This takes alot of ^ff0000dexterity^000000 on the part of the gunslinger.";
			next;
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "Now before ya go running off shooting dem guns in the air, all high fallooti'n and dancing around. Ya need to understand that this isn't an easy job!";
			next;
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "Bullets cost zeny so you need to be sure that everything you shoot is worth the price! We attack at a range so that nasty cur with the pig sticker doesn't rustle your jimmies!";
			next;
			mes "[Lusa]";
			mes "Y'all understand?";
			next;
			while(1) {
				switch(select("Ranged attack?", "Why is ammo expensive?", "What's the Job Change Test?", "Yes~!!")) {
				case 1:
					mes "[Lusa]";
					mes "Some low tech barbarians need both Strength and Dexterity in order to fight properly. This isn't true for gunslingers.";
					next;
					mes "[Lusa]";
					mes "Why our dexterity influences both attack power and accuracy! Remember, talk slowly but think quickly!";
					next;
					break;

		}

iz_ac02,162,86,4	script	Guild Staff#ac	4W_M_02,{
	if (!checkweight(1301,1)) {
		mes "- You are carrying too many items. -";
		close;
	}
	if (nov_3_guns < 8) {
		mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
		mes "Yesssssss? I wass sssent by the academy.";
		close;
	} else if (nov_3_guns > 7) {
		disable_items;
	}
	mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
	mes "I am ^A2563ESharp Snake's Fang^000000 from the Gunslinger Guild. What do you need?";
	next;
	if (select("Exchange Guns", "Just Saying Hello") == 2) {
		mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
		mes "You seem to be that guy our brother mentioned.";
		next;
		mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
		mes "You don't need to worry, he said you're doing great!";
		close2;
		enable_items;
		end;
	}
	mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
	mes "Do you wish to exchange your guild issued weapon?";
	next;
	mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
	mes "Let's first check your gun's condition.";
	next;
	if (getequipname(EQI_HAND_R) == "") {
		mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
		mes "If you want to proceed, you need to have your weapon equipped.";
		close2;
		enable_items;
		end;
	} else {
		.@gun = getequipid(EQI_HAND_R);
	}
	mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
	mes "Let's see...";
	next;
	if (.@gun == 13116) {// Novice_Revolver
		.@gun_code$ = "RV";
		.@now_gun$ = "Revolver";
		mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
		mes "You want to exchange your Guild issued Revolver?";
		next;
	} else if (.@gun == 13180) {// Novice_Rifle
		.@gun_code$ = "RF";
		.@now_gun$ = "Rifle";
		mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
		mes "You want to exchange your Guild issued Rifle?";
		next;
	} else if (.@gun == 13181) {// Novice_Shotgun
		.@gun_code$ = "SG";
		.@now_gun$ = "Shotgun";
		mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
		mes "You want to exchange your Guild issued Shotgun?";
		next;
	} else if (.@gun == 13182) {// Novice_Gatling
		.@gun_code$ = "GT";
		.@now_gun$ = "Gatling";
		mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
		mes "You want to exchange your Guild issued Gatling Gun?";
		next;
	} else if (.@gun == 13183) {// Novice_Grenade_Launcher
		.@gun_code$ = "GL";
		.@now_gun$ = "Grenade Launcher";
		mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
		mes "You want to exchange your Guild issued Grenade Launcher?";
		next;
	} else {
		mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
		mes "The gun you are using was not provided by the guild.";
		close;
	}
	mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
	mes "The gun looks to be in good condition.";
	next;
	mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
	mes "Please select the novice weapon you wish to exchange for your "+.@now_gun$+"!";
	next;
	switch(select("Exchange for Revolver", "Exchange for Rifle", "Exchange for Shotgun", "Exchange for Gatling Gun", "Exchange for Grenade Launcher", "Cancel")) {
	case 1:
		if (.@gun == 13116) {
			mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
			mes "You already have that gun, just use it!";
			close2;
			enable_items;
			end;
		} else {
			delequip EQI_HAND_R;
			getitem 13116,1;// Novice_Revolver
		}
		break;
	case 2:
		if (.@gun == 13180) {
			mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
			mes "You already have that gun, just use it!";
			close2;
			enable_items;
			end;
		} else {
			delequip EQI_HAND_R;
			getitem 13180,1;// Novice_Rifle
		}
		break;
	case 3:
		if (.@gun == 13181) {
			mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
			mes "You already have that gun, just use it!";
			close2;
			enable_items;
			end;
		} else {
			delequip EQI_HAND_R;
			getitem 13181,1;// Novice_Shotgun
		}
		break;
	case 4:
		if (.@gun == 13182) {
			mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
			mes "You already have that gun, just use it!";
			close2;
			enable_items;
			end;
		} else {
			delequip EQI_HAND_R;
			getitem 13182,1;// Novice_Gatling
		}
		break;
	case 5:
		if (.@gun == 13183) {
			mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
			mes "You already have that gun, just use it!";
			close2;
			enable_items;
			end;
		} else {
			delequip EQI_HAND_R;
			getitem 13183,1;// Novice_Grenade_Launcher
		}
		break;
	case 6:
		break;
	}
	mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
	mes "Gun control management number ^FF0000"+.@gun_code$+""+rand(0,9)+""+rand(0,9)+""+rand(0,9)+""+rand(0,9)+""+rand(0,9)+""+rand(0,9)+"^000000.";
	next;
	mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
	mes "Are there any issues?";
	next;
	select("No issues.");
	mes "[Sharp Snake's Fang]";
	mes "Cherish your gun!";

	end;

			erasequest 1230;

iz_ac02,1,1,0	script	#nbacStone01	CLEAR_NPC,{
	end;

OnInit:
	donpcevent "#"+strnpcinfo(2)+"::OnSpawn";
	setcell "iz_ac02",58,142,63,144,cell_icewall,1;// allow monster to drop in area
	end;

OnReset:
	killmonster strnpcinfo(4),"#"+strnpcinfo(2)+"::OnMyMobDead";
	donpcevent "#"+strnpcinfo(2)+"::OnSpawn";
	end;

OnMyMobDead:
	.@dead_num = mobcount(""+strnpcinfo(4)+"", "#"+strnpcinfo(2)+"::OnMyMobDead");
	if (.@dead_num < 1)
		donpcevent "#"+strnpcinfo(2)+"::OnSpawn";
	end;

OnSpawn:
	monster strnpcinfo(4),59,143,"Poring",1725,1,"#"+strnpcinfo(2)+"::OnMyMobDead";
	monster strnpcinfo(4),60,143,"Poring",1725,1,"#"+strnpcinfo(2)+"::OnMyMobDead";
	monster strnpcinfo(4),61,143,"Poring",1725,1,"#"+strnpcinfo(2)+"::OnMyMobDead";
	monster strnpcinfo(4),62,143,"Poring",1725,1,"#"+strnpcinfo(2)+"::OnMyMobDead";
	end;
}

			mes "How are you? Haven't seen you long time.. Please pay more frequent visits and do refining.";
			close;
		case 2:
			mes "[Refinery Owner Han]";
			mes "Just as before, labor-management consensus have achieved.";
			next;
			mes "[Refinery Owner Han]";
			mes "We understand the employees' complaints and prepared the resolutions.";
			next;
			mes "[Refinery Owner Han]";
			mes "Perhaps from that reason, I can hear any other complaints from them.";
			close;
		case 3:
			mes "[Refinery Owner Han]";
			mes "You have a question..";
			next;
			mes "[Refinery Owner Han]";
			mes "But I haven't told you anything in the beginning.";
			next;
			mes "[Refinery Owner Han]";
			mes "It might be better for you to ask questions of the staff you met before.";
			next;
			mes "[Refinery Owner Han]";
			mes "You can ask the explanations concerning ^FD4F02weapon levels^000000 and ^FD4F02saftey refining ^000000, to ^142CEBMr. Tadde^000000, concerning ^FD4F02refining price^000000 and ^FD4F02refining effect^000000, ^142CEBto Mr. Locas^000000.";
			next;
			mes "[Refinery Owner Han]";
			mes "He will give you kind answers.";
			close;
		case 4:
			break;
		}
		close;
	} else {
		mes "[Refinery Owner Han]";
		mes "Something strange must've happened. If this continues, please contact customer service.";
		close;
	}

OnInit:
	questinfo 5153, QTYPE_QUEST, 1;
	setquestinfo_level 5153,1,20;
	end;
}
